;; -*- Mode: Lisp -*-

;; Russian Metaphor Source Axioms
;; Katya Ovchinnikova, Jonathan Gordon


;; A God
;;   A supreme being; to regard or treat as a god; deify; idolize.

;; A God: Type

(B (name god/бог)
   (=> (^ (S#A_GOD e0 :0.45) (SS#A_GOD%TYPE x e0 :0.45))
       (бог-nn e0 x)))
(B (name goddess/богиня)
   (=> (^ (S#A_GOD e0 :0.45) (SS#A_GOD%TYPE x e0 :0.45))
       (богиня-nn e0 x)))
(B (name deity/божество)
   (=> (^ (S#A_GOD e0 :0.45) (SS#A_GOD%TYPE x e0 :0.45))
       (божество-nn e0 x)))
(B (name idol/идол)
   (=> (^ (S#A_GOD e0 :0.45) (SS#A_GOD%TYPE x e0 :0.45))
       (идол-nn e0 x)))

(B (name divine/божеский)
   (=> (^ (S#A_GOD e0 :0.45) (SS#A_GOD%TYPE e0 e0 :0.45))
       (божеский-adj e0 x)))
(B (name godlike/божественный)
   (=> (^ (S#A_GOD e0 :0.45) (SS#A_GOD%TYPE e0 e0 :0.45))
       (божественный-adj e0 x)))

(B (name resurrect/воскреснуть)
   (=> (^ (S#A_GOD e0 :0.45) (SS#A_GOD%TYPE e0 e0 :0.45))
       (воскреснуть-vb e0 x y z)))
(B (name resurrect/воскресать)
   (=> (^ (S#A_GOD e0 :0.45) (SS#A_GOD%TYPE e0 e0 :0.45))
       (воскресать-vb e0 x y z)))


;; A God: Veneration

(B (name worship/поклоняться)
   (=> (^ (S#A_GOD e0 :0.3) (SS#A_GOD%VENERATION e0 e0 :0.3)
          (R#WORSHIP-AGENT x e0 :0.3))
       (поклоняться-vb e0 x y u)))
(B (name bow/преклоняться)
   (=> (^ (S#A_GOD e0 :0.3) (SS#A_GOD%VENERATION e0 e0 :0.3)
          (R#WORSHIP-AGENT x e0 :0.3))
       (преклоняться-vb e0 x y u)))
(B (name bow/кланяться)
   (=> (^ (S#A_GOD e0 :0.3) (SS#A_GOD%VENERATION e0 e0 :0.3)
          (R#WORSHIP-AGENT x e0 :0.3))
       (кланяться-vb e0 x y u)))
(B (name esteem/почитать)
   (=> (^ (S#A_GOD e0 :0.3) (SS#A_GOD%VENERATION e0 e0 :0.3)
          (R#WORSHIP-AGENT x e0 :0.3))
       (почитать-vb e0 x y u)))
(B (name pray/молиться)
   (=> (^ (S#A_GOD e0 :0.3) (SS#A_GOD%VENERATION e0 e0 :0.3)
          (R#WORSHIP-AGENT x e0 :0.3))
       (молиться-vb e0 x y u)))
(B (name preach/проповедовать)
   (=> (^ (S#A_GOD e0 :0.3) (SS#A_GOD%VENERATION e0 e0 :0.3)
          (R#WORSHIP-AGENT x e0 :0.3))
       (проповедовать-vb e0 x y u)))
(B (name deify/обожествлять)
   (=> (^ (S#A_GOD e0 :0.3) (SS#A_GOD%VENERATION e0 e0 :0.3)
          (R#WORSHIP-AGENT x e0 :0.3))
       (обожествлять-vb e0 x y u)))
(B (name deify/обожествить)
   (=> (^ (S#A_GOD e0 :0.3) (SS#A_GOD%VENERATION e0 e0 :0.3)
          (R#WORSHIP-AGENT x e0 :0.3))
       (обожествить-vb e0 x y u)))

(B (name worship/поклонение)
   (=> (^ (S#A_GOD u :0.45) (SS#A_GOD%VENERATION x u :0.45))
       (поклонение-nn e0 x)))
(B (name worship/преклонение)
   (=> (^ (S#A_GOD u :0.45) (SS#A_GOD%VENERATION x u :0.45))
       (преклонение-nn e0 x)))
(B (name deification/обожествление)
   (=> (^ (S#A_GOD u :0.45) (SS#A_GOD%VENERATION x u :0.45))
       (обожествление-nn e0 x)))

(B (name temple/храм)
   (=> (^ (S#A_GOD u :0.45) (SS#A_GOD%VENERATION x u :0.45))
       (храм-nn e0 x)))
(B (name cult/культ)
   (=> (^ (S#A_GOD u :0.45) (SS#A_GOD%VENERATION x u :0.45))
       (культ-nn e0 x)))
(B (name altar/алтарь)
   (=> (^ (S#A_GOD u :0.45) (SS#A_GOD%VENERATION x u :0.45))
       (алтарь-nn e0 x)))
(B (name servant/служитель)
   (=> (^ (S#A_GOD u :0.45) (SS#A_GOD%VENERATION x u :0.45))
       (служитель-nn e0 x)))


;; A God: Mapping

(B (name god-map)
   (=> (I#A_GOD x :0.9)
       (S#A_GOD x)))
(B (name god-type-map)
   (=> (I#A_GOD%TYPE x y :0.9)
       (SS#A_GOD%TYPE x y)))
(B (name god-veneration-map)
   (=> (I#A_GOD%VENERATION x y :0.9)
       (SS#A_GOD%VENERATION x y)))


;; A Right
;;   That which is due to anyone by just claim, legal guarantees, moral
;;   principles, etc.

;; A Right: Type

(B (name right/право)
   (=> (^ (S#A_RIGHT e0 :0.45) (SS#A_RIGHT%TYPE x e0 :0.45))
       (право-nn e0 x)))
(B (name right-to/право-на)
   (=> (^ (S#A_RIGHT e0 :0.45) (SS#A_RIGHT%TYPE x e0 :0.45))
       (^ (право-nn e0 x) (на-in e1 x y))))


;; A Right: Mapping

(B (name a_right-map)
   (=> (I#A_RIGHT x :0.9)
       (S#A_RIGHT x)))
(B (name a_right-type-map)
   (=> (I#A_RIGHT%TYPE x y :0.9)
       (SS#A_RIGHT%TYPE x y)))


;; Abyss
;;   A deep, immeasurable space, gulf, or cavity; vast chasm; anything
;;   profound, unfathomable, or infinite.

;; Abyss: Type

(B (name abyss/пропасть)
   (=> (^ (S#ABYSS e0 :0.45) (SS#ABYSS%TYPE x e0 :0.45))
       (пропасть-nn e0 x)))
(B (name abyss/бездна)
   (=> (^ (S#ABYSS e0 :0.45) (SS#ABYSS%TYPE x e0 :0.45))
       (бездна-nn e0 x)))
(B (name hell/ад)
   (=> (^ (S#ABYSS e0 :0.45) (SS#ABYSS%TYPE x e0 :0.45))
       (ад-nn e0 x)))
(B (name cave/пещера)
   (=> (^ (S#ABYSS e0 :0.45) (SS#ABYSS%TYPE x e0 :0.45))
       (пещера-nn e0 x)))
(B (name hole/дыра)
   (=> (^ (S#ABYSS e0 :0.45) (SS#ABYSS%TYPE x e0 :0.45))
       (дыра-nn e0 x)))
(B (name pit/яма)
   (=> (^ (S#ABYSS e0 :0.45) (SS#ABYSS%TYPE x e0 :0.45))
       (яма-nn e0 x)))
(B (name black-hole/черный-дыра)
   (=> (^ (S#ABYSS e0 :0.45) (SS#ABYSS%TYPE x e0 :0.45))
       (^ (черный-adj e0 x) (дыра-nn e1 x))))
(B (name black-hole/чёрный-дыра)
   (=> (^ (S#ABYSS e0 :0.45) (SS#ABYSS%TYPE x e0 :0.45))
       (^ (чёрный-adj e0 x) (дыра-nn e1 x))))


;; Abyss: Depth

(B (name depth/глубина)
   (=> (^ (S#ABYSS u :0.45) (SS#ABYSS%DEPTH x u :0.45))
       (глубина-nn e0 x)))
(B (name deep/глубокий)
   (=> (^ (S#ABYSS x :0.45) (SS#ABYSS%DEPTH e0 x :0.45))
       (глубокий-adj e0 x)))
(B (name inmost/глубочайший)
   (=> (^ (S#ABYSS x :0.45) (SS#ABYSS%DEPTH e0 x :0.45))
       (глубочайший-adj e0 x)))
(B (name deeper/глубже)
   (=> (^ (S#ABYSS u :0.45) (SS#ABYSS%DEPTH e0 u :0.45))
       (глубже-rb e0 x)))
(B (name bottomless/бездонный)
   (=> (^ (S#ABYSS x :0.45) (SS#ABYSS%DEPTH e0 x :0.45))
       (бездонный-adj e0 x)))
(B (name deepening/углубление)
   (=> (^ (S#ABYSS x :0.45) (SS#ABYSS%DEPTH e0 x :0.45))
       (^ (углубление-nn e0 y) (of-in e1 y x))))

(B (name deepen/углубляться)
   (=> (^ (S#ABYSS x :0.45) (SS#ABYSS%DEPTH e0 x :0.45))
       (углубляться-vb e0 x y z)))
(B (name delve/углубиться)
   (=> (^ (S#ABYSS x :0.45) (SS#ABYSS%DEPTH e0 x :0.45))
       (углубиться-vb e0 x y z)))


;; Abyss: Entrance

(B (name fall-into/провалиться-в)
   (=> (^ (S#ABYSS z :0.3) (SS#ABYSS%ENTRANCE e0 z :0.3)
          (R#ABYSS-THEME x e0 :0.3))
       (^ (провалиться-vb e0 x y u) (в-in e1 e0 z))))
(B (name fall-into/свалиться-в)
   (=> (^ (S#ABYSS z :0.3) (SS#ABYSS%ENTRANCE e0 z :0.3)
          (R#ABYSS-THEME x e0 :0.3))
       (^ (свалиться-vb e0 x y u) (в-in e1 e0 z))))
(B (name fall-into/проваливаться-в)
   (=> (^ (S#ABYSS z :0.3) (SS#ABYSS%ENTRANCE e0 z :0.3)
          (R#ABYSS-THEME x e0 :0.3))
       (^ (проваливаться-vb e0 x y u) (в-in e1 e0 z))))
(B (name push-in/толкнуть-в)
   (=> (^ (S#ABYSS z :0.3) (SS#ABYSS%ENTRANCE e0 z :0.3)
          (R#ABYSS-THEME x e0 :0.3))
       (^ (толкнуть-vb e0 x y u) (в-in e1 e0 z))))
(B (name push-in/столкнуть-в)
   (=> (^ (S#ABYSS z :0.3) (SS#ABYSS%ENTRANCE e0 z :0.3)
          (R#ABYSS-THEME x e0 :0.3))
       (^ (столкнуть-vb e0 x y u) (в-in e1 e0 z))))
(B (name throw-in/бросить-в)
   (=> (^ (S#ABYSS z :0.3) (SS#ABYSS%ENTRANCE e0 z :0.3)
          (R#ABYSS-THEME x e0 :0.3))
       (^ (бросить-vb e0 x y u) (в-in e1 e0 z))))
(B (name throw-in/сбросить-в)
   (=> (^ (S#ABYSS z :0.3) (SS#ABYSS%ENTRANCE e0 z :0.3)
          (R#ABYSS-THEME x e0 :0.3))
       (^ (сбросить-vb e0 x y u) (в-in e1 e0 z))))
(B (name throw-in/кинуть-в)
   (=> (^ (S#ABYSS z :0.3) (SS#ABYSS%ENTRANCE e0 z :0.3)
          (R#ABYSS-THEME x e0 :0.3))
       (^ (кинуть-vb e0 x y u) (в-in e1 e0 z))))
(B (name throw-in/скинуть-в)
   (=> (^ (S#ABYSS z :0.3) (SS#ABYSS%ENTRANCE e0 z :0.3)
          (R#ABYSS-THEME x e0 :0.3))
       (^ (скинуть-vb e0 x y u) (в-in e1 e0 z))))
(B (name slide-into/сползти-в)
   (=> (^ (S#ABYSS z :0.3) (SS#ABYSS%ENTRANCE e0 z :0.3)
          (R#ABYSS-THEME x e0 :0.3))
       (^ (сползти-vb e0 x y u) (в-in e1 e0 z))))
(B (name sliding-in/сползать-в)
   (=> (^ (S#ABYSS z :0.3) (SS#ABYSS%ENTRANCE e0 z :0.3)
          (R#ABYSS-THEME x e0 :0.3))
       (^ (сползать-vb e0 x y u) (в-in e1 e0 z))))

(B (name fail/провалиться)
   (=> (^ (S#ABYSS z :0.3) (SS#ABYSS%ENTRANCE e0 z :0.3)
          (R#ABYSS-THEME x e0 :0.3))
       (провалиться-vb e0 x y u)))
(B (name fall-through/проваливаться)
   (=> (^ (S#ABYSS z :0.3) (SS#ABYSS%ENTRANCE e0 z :0.3)
          (R#ABYSS-THEME x e0 :0.3))
       (проваливаться-vb e0 x y u)))

(B (name balance/балансировать)
   (=> (^ (S#ABYSS z :0.3) (SS#ABYSS%ENTRANCE e0 z :0.3)
          (R#ABYSS-THEME x e0 :0.3))
       (балансировать-vb e0 x y u)))

(B (name edge/край)
   (=> (^ (S#ABYSS u :0.45) (SS#ABYSS%ENTRANCE x u :0.45))
       (край-nn e0 x)))
(B (name verge/грань)
   (=> (^ (S#ABYSS u :0.45) (SS#ABYSS%ENTRANCE x u :0.45))
       (грань-nn e0 x)))


;; Abyss: Exit

(B (name get-out/выбраться-из)
   (=> (^ (S#ABYSS z :0.3) (SS#ABYSS%EXIT e0 z :0.3)
          (R#ABYSS-THEME x e0 :0.3))
       (^ (S#ABYSS e2) (выбраться-vb e0 x y u) (из-in e1 e0 z))))
(B (name get-out/выбираться-из)
   (=> (^ (S#ABYSS z :0.3) (SS#ABYSS%EXIT e0 z :0.3)
          (R#ABYSS-THEME x e0 :0.3))
       (^ (S#ABYSS e2) (выбираться-vb e0 x y u) (из-in e1 e0 z))))
(B (name get-out/выкарабкаться-из)
   (=> (^ (S#ABYSS z :0.3) (SS#ABYSS%EXIT e0 z :0.3)
          (R#ABYSS-THEME x e0 :0.3))
       (^ (выкарабкаться-vb e0 x y u) (из-in e1 e0 z))))
(B (name get-out/вылезти-из)
   (=> (^ (S#ABYSS z :0.3) (SS#ABYSS%EXIT e0 z :0.3)
          (R#ABYSS-THEME x e0 :0.3))
       (^ (вылезти-vb e0 x y u) (из-in e1 e0 z))))
(B (name get-out/вылезать-из)
   (=> (^ (S#ABYSS z :0.3) (SS#ABYSS%EXIT e0 z :0.3)
          (R#ABYSS-THEME x e0 :0.3))
       (^ (вылезать-vb e0 x y u) (из-in e1 e0 z))))
(B (name pull-out/вытащить-из)
   (=> (^ (S#ABYSS z :0.3) (SS#ABYSS%EXIT e0 z :0.3)
          (R#ABYSS-THEME x e0 :0.3))
       (^ (вытащить-vb e0 x y u) (из-in e1 e0 z))))
(B (name pull-out/вытаскивать-из)
   (=> (^ (S#ABYSS z :0.3) (SS#ABYSS%EXIT e0 z :0.3)
          (R#ABYSS-THEME x e0 :0.3))
       (^ (вытаскивать-vb e0 x y u) (из-in e1 e0 z))))
(B (name rise/подняться-из)
   (=> (^ (S#ABYSS z :0.3) (SS#ABYSS%EXIT e0 z :0.3)
          (R#ABYSS-THEME x e0 :0.3))
       (^ (подняться-vb e0 x y u) (из-in e1 e0 z))))
(B (name rise/подниматься-из)
   (=> (^ (S#ABYSS z :0.3) (SS#ABYSS%EXIT e0 z :0.3)
          (R#ABYSS-THEME x e0 :0.3))
       (^ (подниматься-vb e0 x y u) (из-in e1 e0 z))))
(B (name jump-out-of/выскочить-из)
   (=> (^ (S#ABYSS z :0.3) (SS#ABYSS%EXIT e0 z :0.3)
          (R#ABYSS-THEME x e0 :0.3))
       (^ (выскочить-vb e0 x y u) (из-in e1 e0 z))))

(B (name get-out/выкарабкаться)
   (=> (^ (S#ABYSS z :0.3) (SS#ABYSS%EXIT e0 z :0.3)
          (R#ABYSS-THEME x e0 :0.3))
       (выкарабкаться-vb e0 x y u)))
(B (name get-out/вылезти)
   (=> (^ (S#ABYSS z :0.3) (SS#ABYSS%EXIT e0 z :0.3)
          (R#ABYSS-THEME x e0 :0.3))
       (вылезти-vb e0 x y u)))
(B (name get-out/вылезать)
   (=> (^ (S#ABYSS z :0.3) (SS#ABYSS%EXIT e0 z :0.3)
          (R#ABYSS-THEME x e0 :0.3))
       (вылезать-vb e0 x y u)))
(B (name out/выбраться)
   (=> (^ (S#ABYSS z :0.3) (SS#ABYSS%EXIT e0 z :0.3)
          (R#ABYSS-THEME x e0 :0.3))
       (выбраться-vb e0 x y u)))
(B (name get-out/выбираться)
   (=> (^ (S#ABYSS z :0.3) (SS#ABYSS%EXIT e0 z :0.3)
          (R#ABYSS-THEME x e0 :0.3))
       (выбираться-vb e0 x y u)))
(B (name pull/вытащить)
   (=> (^ (S#ABYSS z :0.3) (SS#ABYSS%EXIT e0 z :0.3)

       (вытащить-vb e0 x y u)))
(B (name pull-out/вытаскивать)
   (=> (^ (S#ABYSS z :0.3) (SS#ABYSS%EXIT e0 z :0.3)

(B (name rise/подняться)

       (подниматься-vb e0 x y u)))

   (=> (^ (S#ABYSS z :0.3) (SS#ABYSS%EXIT e0 z :0.3)

       (выскочить-vb e0 x y u)))

(B (name out/выбраться)
   (=> (^ (S#ABYSS z :0.3) (SS#ABYSS%EXIT e0 z :0.3)
          (R#ABYSS-THEME x e0 :0.3))
       (^ (S#ABYSS e1) (выбраться-vb e0 x y u))))
(B (name get-out/выбираться)
   (=> (^ (S#ABYSS z :0.3) (SS#ABYSS%EXIT e0 z :0.3)
          (R#ABYSS-THEME x e0 :0.3))
       (^ (S#ABYSS e1) (выбираться-vb e0 x y u))))


;; Abyss: Mapping

(B (name abyss-map)
   (=> (I#ABYSS x :0.9)
       (S#ABYSS x)))
(B (name abyss-type-map)
   (=> (I#ABYSS%TYPE x e0 :0.9)
       (SS#ABYSS%TYPE x e0)))
(B (name abyss-depth-map)
   (=> (I#ABYSS%DEPTH x y :0.9)
       (SS#ABYSS%DEPTH x y)))
(B (name abyss-entrance-map)
   (=> (I#ABYSS%ENTRANCE x y :0.9)
       (SS#ABYSS%ENTRANCE x y)))
(B (name abyss-exit-map)
   (=> (I#ABYSS%EXIT x y :0.9)
       (SS#ABYSS%EXIT x y)))


;; Accident
;;   An unforeseen and unplanned event or circumstance.

;; Accident: Type

(B (name accident/авария)
   (=> (^ (S#ACCIDENT e0 :0.45) (SS#ACCIDENT%TYPE x e0 :0.45))
       (авария-nn e0 x)))
(B (name disaster/бедствие)
   (=> (^ (S#ACCIDENT e0 :0.45) (SS#ACCIDENT%TYPE x e0 :0.45))
       (бедствие-nn e0 x)))
(B (name disaster/катастрофа)
   (=> (^ (S#ACCIDENT e0 :0.45) (SS#ACCIDENT%TYPE x e0 :0.45))
       (катастрофа-nn e0 x)))
(B (name accident/несчастный-случай)
   (=> (^ (S#ACCIDENT e0 :0.45) (SS#ACCIDENT%TYPE x e0 :0.45))
       (^ (несчастный-adj e1 x) (случай-nn e0 x))))
(B (name catastrophic/катастрофический)
   (=> (^ (S#ACCIDENT e0 :0.45) (SS#ACCIDENT%TYPE e0 e0 :0.45))
       (катастрофический-adj e0 x)))


;; Accident: Mapping

(B (name accident-map)
   (=> (I#ACCIDENT x :0.9)
       (S#ACCIDENT x)))
(B (name accident-type-map)
   (=> (I#ACCIDENT%TYPE x y :0.9)
       (SS#ACCIDENT%TYPE x y)))


;; Addiction
;;   The state of being enslaved to a habit or practice or to something that
;;   is psychologically or physically habit-forming, as narcotics, to such an
;;   extent that its cessation causes severe trauma.

;; Addiction: Type

(B (name narcotic/наркотик)
   (=> (^ (S#ADDICTION e0 :0.3) (SS#ADDICTION%TYPE x e0 :0.3)
          (R#SUBSTANCE x e0 :0.3))
       (наркотик-nn e0 x)))
(B (name cocaine/кокаин)
   (=> (^ (S#ADDICTION e0 :0.3) (SS#ADDICTION%TYPE x e0 :0.3)
          (R#SUBSTANCE x e0 :0.3))
       (кокаин-nn e0 x)))
(B (name alcohol/алкоголь)
   (=> (^ (S#ADDICTION e0 :0.3) (SS#ADDICTION%TYPE x e0 :0.3)
          (R#SUBSTANCE x e0 :0.3))
       (алкоголь-nn e0 x)))
(B (name binge/выпивка)
   (=> (^ (S#ADDICTION e0 :0.3) (SS#ADDICTION%TYPE x e0 :0.3)
          (R#SUBSTANCE x e0 :0.3))
       (выпивка-nn e0 x)))
(B (name vodka/водка)

;; Addiction: Mapping

(B (name addiction-map)
   (=> (I#ADDICTION x :0.9)
       (S#ADDICTION x)))
(B (name addiction-type-map)
   (=> (I#ADDICTION%TYPE x y :0.9)
       (SS#ADDICTION%TYPE x y)))
(B (name addiction-compulsion-map)
   (=> (I#ADDICTION%COMPULSION x y :0.9)
       (SS#ADDICTION%COMPULSION x y)))
(B (name addiction-result-map)
   (=> (I#ADDICTION%RESULT x y :0.9)
       (SS#ADDICTION%RESULT x y)))

   (=> (I#ANIMAL%FUNCTION x y :0.9)
       (SS#ANIMAL%FUNCTION x y)))

   (=> (I#ANIMAL%ACTION x y :0.9)
       (SS#ANIMAL%ACTION x y)))


;; Backward Movement
;;   Movement to or toward what is behind.

(B (name backward/назад)
   (=> (S#BACKWARD_MOVEMENT e0 :0.9)
       (назад-adj e0 x)))
(B (name reverse/обратный)
   (=> (S#BACKWARD_MOVEMENT e0 :0.9)
       (обратный-adj e0 x)))

(B (name reverse/реверсировать)
   (=> (S#BACKWARD_MOVEMENT e0 :0.9)
       (реверсировать-vb e0 x u1 u2)))


;; Backward Movement: Mapping

(B (name backward-movement-map)
   (=> (I#BACKWARD_MOVEMENT x :0.9)
       (S#BACKWARD_MOVEMENT x)))


;; Barrier
;;   Anything used or acting to block someone from going somewhere or from
;;   doing something, or to block something from happening.

(B (name barrier/барьер)
   (=> (S#BARRIER e0 :0.9)
       (барьер-nn e0 x)))
(B (name obstacle/препятствием)
   (=> (S#BARRIER e0 :0.9)
       (препятствием-nn e0 x)))

(B (name block/блокировать)
   (=> (S#BARRIER e0 :0.9)
       (блокировать-vb e0 x0 x1 x2)))


;; Blood Stream
;;   The flowing blood in a circulatory system; a mainstream of power or
;;   vitality. (Formerly BLOOD_SYSTEM.)

;; Blood Stream: Component

(B (name blood/кровь)
   (=> (^ (S#BLOOD_STREAM e0 :0.3) (SS#BLOOD_STREAM%COMPONENT x e0 :0.3)
          (R#BLOOD x e0 :0.3))
       (кровь-nn e0 x)))
(B (name bloodstream/кровоток)
   (=> (^ (S#BLOOD_STREAM e0 :0.3) (SS#BLOOD_STREAM%COMPONENT x e0 :0.3)
          (R#BLOOD x e0 :0.3))
       (кровь-nn e0 x)))
(B (name vein/вена)
   (=> (^ (S#BLOOD_STREAM e0 :0.45) (SS#BLOOD_STREAM%COMPONENT x e0 :0.45))
       (вена-nn e0 x)))
(B (name artery/артерия)
   (=> (^ (S#BLOOD_STREAM e0 :0.45) (SS#BLOOD_STREAM%COMPONENT x e0 :0.45))
       (артерия-nn e0 x)))
(B (name blood-system/кровеносный-система)
   (=> (^ (S#BLOOD_STREAM e0 :0.45) (SS#BLOOD_STREAM%COMPONENT x e0 :0.45))
       (^ (кровеносный-adj e0 x) (система-nn e1 x))))


;; Blood Stream: Movement

(B (name flow/течь)
   (=> (^ (S#BLOOD_STREAM e0 :0.45) (SS#BLOOD_STREAM%MOVEMENT e1 e0 :0.45))
       (^ (течь-vb e1 x y u) (SS#BLOOD_STREAM%COMPONENT x e0))))
(B (name flow/струиться)
   (=> (^ (S#BLOOD_STREAM e0 :0.45) (SS#BLOOD_STREAM%MOVEMENT e1 e0 :0.45))
       (^ (струиться-vb e1 x y u) (SS#BLOOD_STREAM%COMPONENT x e0))))

(B (name circulation/кровообращение)
   (=> (^ (S#BLOOD_STREAM e0 :0.45) (SS#BLOOD_STREAM%MOVEMENT x e0 :0.45))
       (кровообращение-nn e1 x)))


;; Blood Stream: Mapping

(B (name blood-stream-map)
   (=> (I#BLOOD_STREAM x :0.9)
       (S#BLOOD_STREAM x)))
(B (name blood-stream-component-map)
   (=> (I#BLOOD_STREAM%COMPONENT x y :0.9)
       (SS#BLOOD_STREAM%COMPONENT x y)))
(B (name blood-stream-movement-map)
   (=> (I#BLOOD_STREAM%MOVEMENT x y :0.9)
       (SS#BLOOD_STREAM%MOVEMENT x y)))

       (SS#CONFINEMENT%EXIT x y)))

   (=> (^ (S#DARKNESS e0 :0.3)

;; Darkness: Mapping

(B (name darkness-map)
   (=> (I#DARKNESS x :0.9)
       (S#DARKNESS x)))
(B (name dark-end-of-range-map)
   (=> (I#DARKNESS%DARK_END_OF_RANGE_OF_DARKNESS_LIGHT x y :0.9)
       (SS#DARKNESS%DARK_END_OF_RANGE_OF_DARKNESS_LIGHT x y)))
(B (name darkness-movementmap)
   (=> (I#DARKNESS%MOVEMENT x y :0.9)
       (SS#DARKNESS%MOVEMENT x y)))


;; Disease
;;   A disordered or incorrectly functioning organ, part, structure, or system
;;   of the body resulting from the effect of genetic or developmental errors,
;;   infection, poisons, nutritional deficiency or imbalance, toxicity, or
;;   unfavorable environmental factors; illness; sickness; ailment.

;; Disease: Mapping

(B (name disease-map)
   (=> (I#DISEASE e0 :0.9)
       (S#DISEASE x)))
(B (name disease-type-map)
   (=> (I#DISEASE%TYPE x y :0.9)
       (SS#DISEASE%TYPE x y)))
(B (name disease-cure-map)
   (=> (I#DISEASE%CURE x y :0.9)
       (SS#DISEASE%CURE x y)))
(B (name disease-treatment-map)
   (=> (I#DISEASE%TREATMENT x y :0.9)
       (SS#DISEASE%TREATMENT x y)))

   (=> (I#DISEASE%SYMPTOMS x y :0.9)

;; Movement: Mapping

(B (name movement-map)
   (=> (I#MOVEMENT x :0.9)
       (S#MOVEMENT x)))
(B (name movement-movement-map)
   (=> (I#MOVEMENT%MOVEMENT x y :0.9)
       (SS#MOVEMENT%MOVEMENT x y)))


;; Natural Physical Force
;;   Uncontrollable force of nature that poses potential harm; [nature: all
;;   the animals and plants in the world and all the features, forces, and
;;   processes that exist or happen independently of people, such as the
;;   weather, the sea, mountains, reproduction, and growth]; circumstances
;;   beyond one's control; a any event or force of nature that has
;;   catastrophic consequences, such as avalanche, earthquake, flood, forest
;;   fire, hurricane, lightning, tornado, tsunami, and volcanic eruption.

;; Natural Physical Force: Type

(B (name force/force)
   (=> (^ (S#NATURAL_PHYSICAL_FORCE e0 :0.45)
          (SS#NATURAL_PHYSICAL_FORCE%TYPE x e0 :0.45))
       (сила-nn e0 x)))

;; Obesity
;;   A condition characterized by the excessive accumulation and storage of
;;   fat in the body; Excessive body fat. It is usually caused by sedentary
;;   habits and a diet high in fat, alcohol, or total calories.

;; Physical Burden: Mapping

(B (name physical-burden-map)
   (=> (I#PHYSICAL_BURDEN  e0 :0.9)
       (S#PHYSICAL_BURDEN x)))
(B (name weight-map)
   (=> (I#PHYSICAL_BURDEN%WEIGHT  x y :0.9)
       (SS#PHYSICAL_BURDEN%WEIGHT x y)))
(B (name relief-map)
   (=> (I#PHYSICAL_BURDEN%RELIEF  x y :0.9)
       (SS#PHYSICAL_BURDEN%RELIEF x y)))
(B (name physical-distress-map)
   (=> (I#PHYSICAL_BURDEN%PHYSICAL_DISTRESS  x y :0.9)
       (SS#PHYSICAL_BURDEN%xPHYSICAL_DISTRESS x y)))

   (=> (^ (S#STRUGGLE e0 :0.45) (SS#STRUGGLE%TYPE x e0 :0.45))

;; Upward Movement
;;   Movement from a lower place or level to a higher place or level.
;;   (Including axioms from LOW_POINT%MOVEMENT_UPWARD.)

(B (name climb/подниматься)
   (=> (^ (S#UPWARD_MOVEMENT e0 :0.30) (R#MOVE-U-PATIENT x e0 :0.30))
       (подниматься-vb e0 x y z)))
(B (name jump/прыгать)
   (=> (^ (S#UPWARD_MOVEMENT e0 :0.30) (R#MOVE-U-PATIENT x e0 :0.30))
       (прыгать-vb e0 x y z)))
(B (name raise/поднимать)
   (=> (^ (S#UPWARD_MOVEMENT e0 :0.30) (R#MOVE-UP e0 e0 :0.30)
          (R#MOVER x e0 :0.30))
       (поднимать-vb e0 x y u)))


;; Upward Movement: Mapping

(B (name upward-movement-map)
   (=> (I#UPWARD_MOVEMENT x :0.9)
       (S#UPWARD_MOVEMENT x)))
